## Testes de Qualidade Avançados

```sql
-- models/tests/test_user_engagement.sql
{{
  config(tags = ['data_quality'])
}}

-- Teste de completude: todos os usuários ativos devem ter pelo menos um projeto
WITH active_users AS (
  SELECT user_id
  FROM {{ ref('stg_users') }}
  WHERE user_status = 'active'
)

SELECT
  COUNT(DISTINCT u.user_id) AS active_users_without_projects
FROM active_users u
LEFT JOIN {{ ref('stg_projects') }} p ON u.user_id = p.user_id
WHERE p.project_id IS NULL
```

```sql
-- models/tests/test_project_metrics.sql
{{
  config(tags = ['data_quality'])
}}

-- Teste de consistência: a soma de projetos por status deve bater com o total
WITH status_counts AS (
  SELECT
    COUNT(*) AS total_projects,
    SUM(CASE WHEN project_status = 'draft' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS draft_count,
    SUM(CASE WHEN project_status = 'in_progress' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS in_progress_count,
    SUM(CASE WHEN project_status = 'completed' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS completed_count,
    SUM(CASE WHEN project_status = 'archived' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS archived_count
  FROM {{ ref('stg_projects') }}
)

SELECT
  total_projects,
  (draft_count + in_progress_count + completed_count + archived_count) AS sum_status_counts,
  total_projects - (draft_count + in_progress_count + completed_count + archived_count) AS difference
FROM status_counts
WHERE total_projects != (draft_count + in_progress_count + completed_count + archived_count)
```

## Conclusão

Esta implementação:

1. **Estrutura em Camadas**: Separação clara entre dados brutos, limpos e prontos para consumo
2. **Testes de Qualidade**: Garantia de integridade em todas as camadas
3. **Otimizações**: Particionamento, clustering e materialized views para consultas complexas
4. **Documentação**: Catálogo completo com linhagem e SLAs
5. **Migração Segura**: Processo controlado com validações
6. **Automação**: Orquestração com Airflow e transformações com dbt

A estrutura proposta permite:
- Consultas analíticas complexas com melhor performance
- Rastreabilidade completa dos dados
- Atualizações incrementais eficientes
- Governança e compliance integrados
- Escalabilidade para novos domínios e métricas

Próximos passos:
1. Implementar os dashboards no Metabase/Grafana
2. Configurar alertas para SLAs e testes de qualidade
3. Documentar processos de manutenção e evolução
4. Treinar a squad nos novos datasets e métricas disponíveis

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
Para implementar automações de monitoramento e auto-recuperação na V9 Core, garantindo estabilidade 100% autônoma com alertas proativos e resolução automática de incidentes, podemos usar uma combinação de ferramentas de observabilidade, automação de operações e orquestração de recuperação de falhas.

Vamos focar em um sistema básico que inclui:

1. **Monitoramento com Prometheus e Grafana**: Para capturar e visualizar métricas em tempo real.
2. **Automação com Alertmanager**: Para definir alertas proativos com regras detalhadas.
3. **Auto-recuperação com scripts de orquestração**: Para executar ações de recuperação automática diante de incidentes.

### Estrutura do Projeto

Teremos as seguintes pastas:

- `src/`: Contém scripts de automação e orquestração.
- `monitoring/`: Configurações de Prometheus, Grafana e Alertmanager.
- `public/`: Interface básica index.html para visualização de status geral da V9 Core.

### Código Completo

#### 1. `docker-compose.yml`

Para criar contêineres de Prometheus, Grafana e Alertmanager:

```yaml
version: '3.7'

services:
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    volumes:
      - grafana-storage:/var/lib/grafana

  alertmanager:
    image: prom/alertmanager:latest
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/alertmanager.yml:/etc/alertmanager/alertmanager.yml
    ports:
      - "9093:9093"

volumes:
  grafana-storage:
```

#### 2. `monitoring/prometheus.yml`

Configuração do Prometheus para monitorar a aplicação e Alertmanager:

```yaml
global:
  scrape_interval: 15s

scrape_configs:
  - job_name: 'v9_core'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['localhost:your_app_port']

  - job_name: 'alertmanager'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['alertmanager:9093']
```

#### 3. `monitoring/alertmanager.yml`

Configuração do Alertmanager para enviar alertas:

```yaml
global:
  resolve_timeout: 5m

route:
  receiver: 'default-receiver'

receivers:
  - name: 'default-receiver'
    email_configs:
      - to: 'your_email@example.com'
        from: 'alertmanager@example.com'
        smarthost: 'smtp.example.com:587'
        auth_username: 'alertmanager@example.com'
        auth_identity: 'alertmanager@example.com'
        auth_password: 'yourpassword'
```

#### 4. `src/auto_recovery.sh`

Script para auto-recuperação:

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# Comando para restartar o serviço V9 Core
restart_service() {
  echo "Restarting V9 Core service..."
  # Exemplo de restart de um serviço:
  systemctl restart v9_core_service
}

# Lógica simples para detectar quando um restart é necessário
if ! systemctl is-active --quiet v9_core_service; then
  restart_service
fi
```

#### 5. `public/index.html`

Interface básica para visualização de status:

```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>Status Monitor</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.1.3/dist/css/bootstrap.min.css">
</head>
<body>
    <div class="container mt-5">
        <h1>V9 Core Status Monitor</h1>
        <p>Use the links below to access monitoring dashboards:</p>
        <ul>
            <li><a href="http://localhost:9090" target="_blank">Prometheus</a></li>
            <li><a href="http://localhost:3000" target="_blank">Grafana</a></li>
            <li><a href="http://localhost:9093" target="_blank">Alertmanager</a></li>
        </ul>
    </div>
</body>
</html>
```

### Instruções de Uso

1. **Configuração**: Atualize os arquivos de configuração com as informações relevantes, como `localhost:your_app_port` e o seu email `your_email@example.com`.
2. **Inicialize o ambiente**: Execute `docker-compose up -d` para subir o ambiente de monitoramento.
3. **Monitoramento**: Acesse os dashboards de Prometheus, Grafana e Alertmanager através dos links fornecidos na interface web.
4. **Auto-recuperação**: Configure o `auto_recovery.sh` para rodar periodicamente via cron job para garantir que o serviço V9 Core esteja sempre ativo.

Esse setup básico permitirá o monitoramento e auto-recuperação autônoma do V9 Core, garantindo alertas proativos e respostas rápidas a incidentes. Ajuste e expanda o script de recuperação e as regras de alerta conforme necessário para o ambiente real.

## Implementação Completa

### 1. Configuração Base (config.js)

```javascript
// src/config.js
module.exports = {
  // SLO Configuration
  SLO: {
    AVAILABILITY: 0.9999, // 99.99%
    LATENCY_P95: 300, // ms
    ERROR_RATE: 0.001, // 0.1%
    LLM_LATENCY_P95: 8000, // ms
    HEALTH_CHECK_INTERVAL: 30000, // 30s
    ERROR_BUDGET_WINDOW: 30 // days
  },

  // Canary Configuration
  CANARY: {
    TRAFFIC_PERCENTAGE: 5, // 5% of traffic to canary
    RAMP_UP_INTERVAL: 300000, // 5 minutes
    MAX_TRAFFIC: 50, // 50% max canary traffic
    STABILITY_THRESHOLD: 0.999, // 99.9% success rate
    LATENCY_THRESHOLD: 1.2, // 20% worse than baseline
    MONITORING_WINDOW: 300000 // 5 minutes
  },

  // Rollback Configuration
  ROLLBACK: {
    AUTOMATIC_TRIGGER_THRESHOLD: 0.01, // 1% error rate increase
    MANUAL_TRIGGER_WINDOW: 900000, // 15 minutes
    HEALTH_CHECK_RETRIES: 3,
    ROLLBACK_TIMEOUT: 300000 // 5 minutes
  },

  // Monitoring
  MONITORING: {
    METRICS_INTERVAL: 10000, // 10s
    ALERT_THRESHOLD: 0.005, // 0.5% error rate
    INCIDENT_SEVERITY: {
      SEV1: { threshold: 0.1, responseTime: 300000 }, // 10% error, 5min response
      SEV2: { threshold: 0.05, responseTime: 900000 }, // 5% error, 15min response
      SEV3: { threshold: 0.01, responseTime: 3600000 }, // 1% error, 1h response
      SEV4: { threshold: 0.005, responseTime: 86400000 } // 0.5% error, 24h response
    }
  },

  // Infrastructure
  INFRA: {
    PRIMARY_REGION: 'us-east-1',
    SECONDARY_REGION: 'us-west-2',
    MIN_INSTANCES: 3,
    MAX_INSTANCES: 10,
    AUTOSCALE_THRESHOLD: 0.7 // 70% CPU
  },

  // LLM Gateway
  LLM_GATEWAY: {
    PROVIDERS: ['claude', 'gemini', 'gpt'],
    FALLBACK_STRATEGY: 'round-robin',
    QUOTA_THRESHOLD: 0.9 // 90% of quota
  }
};
```

### 2. Canary Deployment System

```javascript
// src/canary/canary-deployer.js
const { CANARY } = require('../config');
const { log } = require('../monitoring/observability');
const TrafficRouter = require('../load-balancing/traffic-router');

class CanaryDeployer {
  constructor() {
    this.currentVersion = null;
    this.canaryVersion = null;
    this.trafficPercentage = CANARY.TRAFFIC_PERCENTAGE;
    this.isDeploying = false;
    this.monitoringInterval = null;
    this.trafficRouter = new TrafficRouter();
  }

  async startCanaryDeployment(version) {
    if (this.isDeploying) {
      throw new Error('Canary deployment already in progress');
    }

    this.canaryVersion = version;
    this.isDeploying = true;
    log(`Starting canary deployment for version ${version} with ${this.trafficPercentage}% traffic`);

    // Start monitoring
    this.startMonitoring();

    // Gradually increase traffic
    this.rampUpTraffic();
  }

  async rampUpTraffic() {
    const rampUp = setInterval(async () => {
      if (this.trafficPercentage >= CANARY.MAX_TRAFFIC) {
        clearInterval(rampUp);
        log('Canary deployment reached maximum traffic percentage');
        return;
      }

      this.trafficPercentage = Math.min(
        this.trafficPercentage + CANARY.TRAFFIC_PERCENTAGE,
        CANARY.MAX_TRAFFIC
      );

      log(`Increasing canary traffic to ${this.trafficPercentage}%`);

      // Check stability before continuing
      const isStable = await this.checkStability();
      if (!isStable) {
        clearInterval(rampUp);
        await this.rollbackCanary();
      }
    }, CANARY.RAMP_UP_INTERVAL);
  }

  async checkStability() {
    // Implement stability checks based on error rates, latency, etc.
    const metrics = await this.trafficRouter.getCanaryMetrics();
    const successRate = metrics.successRate;
    const latencyRatio = metrics.latency / metrics.baselineLatency;

    if (successRate < CANARY.STABILITY_THRESHOLD) {
      log(`Canary stability check failed: success rate ${successRate} below threshold`);
      return false;
    }

    if (latencyRatio > CANARY.LATENCY_THRESHOLD) {
      log(`Canary stability check failed: latency ${latencyRatio}x baseline`);
      return false;
    }

    return true;
  }

  async promoteCanary() {
    if (!this.isDeploying) {
      throw new Error('No canary deployment in progress');
    }

    const isStable = await this.checkStability();
    if (!isStable) {
      log('Cannot promote unstable canary deployment');
      return false;
    }

    this.currentVersion = this.canaryVersion;
    this.trafficPercentage = 0;
    this.canaryVersion = null;
    this.isDeploying = false;

    clearInterval(this.monitoringInterval);
    log(`Canary deployment promoted to version ${this.currentVersion}`);

    return true;
  }

  async rollbackCanary() {
    if (!this.isDeploying) {
      throw new Error('No canary deployment in progress');
    }

    this.trafficPercentage = 0;
    this.canaryVersion = null;
    this.isDeploying = false;

    clearInterval(this.monitoringInterval);
    log('Canary deployment rolled back');

    return true;
  }

  startMonitoring() {
    this.monitoringInterval = setInterval(async () => {
      const metrics = await this.trafficRouter.getCanaryMetrics();
      log(`Canary metrics - Success: ${metrics.successRate}, Latency: ${metrics.latency}ms`);

      // Check for automatic rollback conditions
      if (metrics.errorRate > CANARY.AUTOMATIC_ROLLBACK_THRESHOLD) {
        log('Automatic rollback triggered due to high error rate');
        await this.rollbackCanary();
      }
    }, CANARY.MONITORING_WINDOW);
  }
}

module.exports = CanaryDeployer;
```

```javascript
// src/canary/canary-router.js
const { CANARY } = require('../config');
const { getCurrentMetrics } = require('../monitoring/observability');

class CanaryRouter {
  constructor() {
    this.currentVersion = 'v1.0.0';
    this.canaryVersion = null;
    this.trafficPercentage = 0;
  }

  async routeRequest(req) {
    const metrics = getCurrentMetrics();
    const shouldRouteToCanary = Math.random() * 100 < this.trafficPercentage;

    if (shouldRouteToCanary && this.canaryVersion) {
      // Add canary headers for observability
      req.headers['x-canary-version'] = this.canaryVersion;
      req.headers['x-canary-traffic'] = this.trafficPercentage;

      // Track canary metrics
      metrics.canaryRequests++;
      return { version: this.canaryVersion, isCanary: true };
    }

    // Track baseline metrics
    metrics.baselineRequests++;
    return { version: this.currentVersion, isCanary: false };
  }

  updateCanaryConfig(version, percentage) {
    this.canaryVersion = version;
    this.trafficPercentage = percentage;
  }

  getCanaryMetrics() {
    const metrics = getCurrentMetrics();
    return {
      successRate: metrics.canarySuccessRate,
      errorRate: metrics.canaryErrorRate,
      latency: metrics.canaryLatency,
      baselineLatency: metrics.baselineLatency,
      trafficPercentage: this.trafficPercentage
    };
  }
}

module.exports = CanaryRouter;
```

```javascript
// src/canary/canary-monitor.js
const { CANARY } = require('../config');
const { log, getCurrentMetrics } = require('../monitoring/observability');
const RollbackManager = require('../rollback/rollback-manager');

class CanaryMonitor {
  constructor() {
    this.rollbackManager = new RollbackManager();
    this.monitoringInterval = null;
  }

  startMonitoring() {
    this.monitoringInterval = setInterval(async () => {
      const metrics = getCurrentMetrics();
      const canaryMetrics = this.getCanaryMetrics();

      // Check for SLO violations
      if (canaryMetrics.errorRate > CANARY.ALERT_THRESHOLD) {
        log(`Canary error rate ${canaryMetrics.errorRate} exceeds threshold`);
        await this.handleCanaryFailure();
      }

      if (canaryMetrics.latency > CANARY.LATENCY_THRESHOLD * metrics.baselineLatency) {
        log(`Canary latency ${canaryMetrics.latency}ms exceeds threshold`);
        await this.handleCanaryFailure();
      }

      // Check for error budget consumption
      if (metrics.errorBudgetConsumed > 0.8) {
        log('Error budget consumption high, pausing canary');
        await this.pauseCanary();
      }
    }, CANARY.MONITORING_WINDOW);
  }

  getCanaryMetrics() {
    const metrics = getCurrentMetrics();
    return {
      successRate: metrics.canarySuccessRate,
      errorRate: metrics.canaryErrorRate,
      latency: metrics.canaryLatency,
      trafficPercentage: metrics.canaryTrafficPercentage
    };
  }

  async handleCanaryFailure() {
    log('Canary failure detected, initiating rollback');
    await this.rollbackManager.triggerRollback('canary-failure');
    this.stopMonitoring();
  }

  async pauseCanary() {
    log('Pausing canary deployment due to high error budget consumption');
    // Implementation to pause canary traffic
  }

  stopMonitoring() {
    if (this.monitoringInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.monitoringInterval);
    }
  }
}

module.exports = CanaryMonitor;
```

### 3. Rollback System

```javascript
// src/rollback/rollback-manager.js
const { ROLLBACK } = require('../config');
const { log, getCurrentMetrics } = require('../monitoring/observability');
const CanaryDeployer = require('../canary/canary-deployer');
const HealthChecker = require('../load-balancing/health-checker');

class RollbackManager {
  constructor() {
    this.canaryDeployer = new CanaryDeployer();
    this.healthChecker = new HealthChecker();
    this.rollbackInProgress = false;
    this.rollbackTimeout = null;
  }

  async triggerRollback(reason) {
    if (this.rollbackInProgress) {
      log('Rollback already in progress');
      return false;
    }

    this.rollbackInProgress = true;
    log(`Rollback triggered: ${reason}`);

    // Set timeout for rollback completion
    this.rollbackTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
      log('Rollback timeout reached, forcing completion');
      this.completeRollback();
    }, ROLLBACK.ROLLBACK_TIMEOUT);

    try {
      // Check if we're in a canary deployment
      if (this.canaryDeployer.isDeploying) {
        await this.canaryDeployer.rollbackCanary();
      }

      // Perform full rollback
      await this.performRollback();

      // Verify rollback success
      const isHealthy = await this.verifyRollback();
      if (!isHealthy) {
        log('Rollback verification failed, manual intervention required');
        return false;
      }

      log('Rollback completed successfully');
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      log(`Rollback failed: ${error.message}`);
      return false;
    } finally {
      this.completeRollback();
    }
  }

  async performRollback() {
    log('Performing rollback to previous stable version');

    // Implementation would depend on deployment system
    // This is a placeholder for the actual rollback logic
    await this.executeRollbackScript();

    // Wait for health checks to pass
    const isHealthy = await this.healthChecker.waitForHealthy(
      ROLLBACK.HEALTH_CHECK_RETRIES
    );

    if (!isHealthy) {
      throw new Error('Health checks failed after rollback');
    }
  }

  async executeRollbackScript() {
    // In a real implementation, this would call the rollback script
    log('Executing rollback script...');
    // Simulate rollback
    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 2000));
    log('Rollback script completed');
  }

  async verifyRollback() {
    log('Verifying rollback success');

    // Check system health
    const isHealthy = await this.healthChecker.isSystemHealthy();
    if (!isHealthy) {
      return false;
    }

    // Check error rates
    const metrics = getCurrentMetrics();
    if (metrics.errorRate > ROLLBACK.AUTOMATIC_TRIGGER_THRESHOLD) {
      return false;
    }

    return true;
  }

  completeRollback() {
    this.rollbackInProgress = false;
    if (this.rollbackTimeout) {
      clearTimeout(this.rollbackTimeout);
    }
  }

  async shouldTriggerAutomaticRollback() {
    const metrics = getCurrentMetrics();

    // Check error rate increase
    if (metrics.errorRate > ROLLBACK.AUTOMATIC_TRIGGER_THRESHOLD) {
      return true;
    }

    // Check latency increase
    if (metrics.latency > 1.5 * metrics.baselineLatency) {
      return true;
    }

    // Check SLO violations
    if (metrics.sloViolations > 0) {
      return true;
    }

    return false;
  }
}

module.exports = RollbackManager;
```

```javascript
// src/rollback/rollback-strategies.js
const { ROLLBACK } = require('../config');
const { log } = require('../monitoring/observability');

class RollbackStrategies {
  constructor() {
    this.strategies = {
      'canary-failure': this.canaryFailureRollback.bind(this),
      'slo-violation': this.sloViolationRollback.bind(this),
      'health-check-failure': this.healthCheckFailureRollback.bind(this),
      'manual-trigger': this.manualTriggerRollback.bind(this)
    };
  }

  async executeStrategy(reason) {
    const strategy = this.strategies[reason];
    if (!strategy) {
      throw new Error(`No rollback strategy for reason: ${reason}`);
    }

    return strategy();
  }

  async canaryFailureRollback() {
    log('Executing canary failure rollback strategy');
    // Implementation specific to canary failures
    return {
      type: 'partial',
      target: 'canary',
      steps: [
        'Stop canary traffic',
        'Verify baseline stability',
        'Analyze canary metrics'
      ]
    };
  }

  async sloViolationRollback() {
    log('Executing SLO violation rollback strategy');
    // Implementation specific to SLO violations
    return {
      type: 'full',
      target: 'all',
      steps: [
        'Identify violating version',
        'Rollback to last known good version',
        'Verify SLO compliance'
      ]
    };
  }

  async healthCheckFailureRollback() {
    log('Executing health check failure rollback strategy');
    // Implementation specific to health check failures
    return {
      type: 'full',
      target: 'all',
      steps: [
        'Check system resources',
        'Verify dependent services',
        'Rollback if no immediate fix available'
      ]
    };
  }

  async manualTriggerRollback() {
    log('Executing manual trigger rollback strategy');
    // Implementation for manual rollbacks
    return {
      type: 'full',
      target: 'all',
      steps: [
        'Verify rollback necessity',
        'Notify stakeholders',
        'Execute rollback'
      ]
    };
  }
}

module.exports = RollbackStrategies;
```

### 4. Monitoring and Observability

```javascript
// src/monitoring/slo-monitor.js
const { SLO } = require('../config');
const { log, recordMetric } = require('./observability');
const IncidentManager = require('./incident-manager');

class SLOMonitor {
  constructor() {
    this.incidentManager = new IncidentManager();
    this.monitoringInterval = null;
    this.errorBudget = 1.0;
    this.lastErrorBudgetUpdate = Date.now();
  }

  startMonitoring() {
    this.monitoringInterval = setInterval(async () => {
      await this.checkSLOs();
      await this.updateErrorBudget();
    }, SLO.HEALTH_CHECK_INTERVAL);
  }

  async checkSLOs() {
    const metrics = this.getCurrentMetrics();

    // Check availability SLO
    if (metrics.availability < SLO.AVAILABILITY) {
      log(`SLO Violation: Availability ${metrics.availability} < ${SLO.AVAILABILITY}`);
      await this.handleSLOViolation('availability', metrics.availability);
    }

    // Check latency SLO
    if (metrics.latencyP95 > SLO.LATENCY_P95) {
      log(`SLO Violation: Latency P95 ${metrics.latencyP95} > ${SLO.LATENCY_P95}`);
      await this.handleSLOViolation('latency', metrics.latencyP95);
    }

    // Check error rate SLO
    if (metrics.errorRate > SLO.ERROR_RATE) {
      log(`SLO Violation: Error rate ${metrics.errorRate} > ${SLO.ERROR_RATE}`);
      await this.handleSLOViolation('errorRate', metrics.errorRate);
    }

    // Check LLM latency SLO
    if (metrics.llmLatencyP95 > SLO.LLM_LATENCY_P95) {
      log(`SLO Violation: LLM Latency P95 ${metrics.llmLatencyP95} > ${SLO.LLM_LATENCY_P95}`);
      await this.handleSLOViolation('llmLatency', metrics.llmLatencyP95);
    }
  }

  async handleSLOViolation(type, value) {
    // Record the violation
    recordMetric('sloViolations', 1);

    // Determine severity
    const severity = this.determineSeverity(type, value);

    // Create incident if needed
    if (severity === 'Sev1' || severity === 'Sev2') {
      await this.incidentManager.createIncident({
        type: `SLO Violation - ${type}`,
        severity,
        description: `SLO violation detected: ${type} = ${value}`,
        metrics: { [type]: value }
      });
    }
  }

  determineSeverity(type, value) {
    // Simple severity determination - would be more sophisticated in production
    const thresholds = {
      availability: {
        Sev1: SLO.AVAILABILITY * 0.99, // 1% below SLO
        Sev2: SLO.AVAILABILITY * 0.995 // 0.5% below SLO
      },
      latency: {
        Sev1: SLO.LATENCY_P95 * 1.5, // 50% above SLO
        Sev2: SLO.LATENCY_P95 * 1.2 // 20% above SLO
      },
      errorRate: {
        Sev1: SLO.ERROR_RATE * 10, // 10x SLO
        Sev2: SLO.ERROR_RATE * 5 // 5x SLO
      },
      llmLatency: {
        Sev1: SLO.LLM_LATENCY_P95 * 1.5, // 50% above SLO
        Sev2: SLO.LLM_LATENCY_P95 * 1.2 // 20% above SLO
      }
    };

    if (value <= thresholds[type].Sev1) {
      return 'Sev1';
    } else if (value <= thresholds[type].Sev2) {
      return 'Sev2';
    } else {
      return 'Sev3';
    }
  }

  async updateErrorBudget() {
    const now = Date.now();
    const timeElapsed = (now - this.lastErrorBudgetUpdate) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24); // in days
    const metrics = this.getCurrentMetrics();

    // Calculate error budget consumption
    const availabilityConsumption = (1 - metrics.availability) * timeElapsed;
    const errorRateConsumption = metrics.errorRate * timeElapsed;

    // Update error budget
    this.errorBudget -= (availabilityConsumption + errorRateConsumption);
    this.errorBudget = Math.max(0, this.errorBudget);
    this.lastErrorBudgetUpdate = now;

    // Record error budget
    recordMetric('errorBudget', this.errorBudget);

    // Check error budget status
    await this.checkErrorBudgetStatus();
  }

  async checkErrorBudgetStatus() {
    if (this.errorBudget <= 0) {
      log('Error budget exhausted!');
      await this.incidentManager.createIncident({
        type: 'Error Budget Exhausted',
        severity: 'Sev1',
        description: 'Error budget has been exhausted',
        metrics: { errorBudget: this.errorBudget }
      });
    } else if (this.errorBudget < 0.2) {
      log('Error budget critical!');
      await this.incidentManager.createIncident({
        type: 'Error Budget Critical',
        severity: 'Sev2',
        description: 'Error budget is below 20%',
        metrics: { errorBudget: this.errorBudget }
      });
    }
  }

  getCurrentMetrics() {
    // In a real implementation, this would fetch from monitoring system
    return {
      availability: 0.99995, // Example value
      latencyP95: 250, // ms
      errorRate: 0.0005, // 0.05%
      llmLatencyP95: 7500, // ms
      canarySuccessRate: 0.9998,
      canaryErrorRate: 0.0002,
      canaryLatency: 280,
      baselineLatency: 250,
      canaryTrafficPercentage: 5
    };
  }

  stopMonitoring() {
    if (this.monitoringInterval) {
      clearInterval(this.monitoringInterval);
    }
  }
}

module.exports = SLOMonitor;
```

```javascript
// src/monitoring/error-budget.js
const { SLO } = require('../config');
const { log, recordMetric } = require('./observability');
const IncidentManager = require('./incident-manager');

class ErrorBudget {
  constructor() {
    this.budget = 1.0; // Start with 100% error budget
    this.windowStart = Date.now();
    this.incidentManager = new IncidentManager();
  }

  consumeBudget(amount, reason) {
    this.budget -= amount;
    this.budget = Math.max(0, this.budget);

    recordMetric('errorBudgetConsumed', amount);
    log(`Error budget consumed: ${amount.toFixed(6)} (${reason}) - Remaining: ${this.budget.toFixed(6)}`);

    this.checkBudgetStatus();
  }

  checkBudgetStatus() {
    if (this.budget <= 0) {
      log('Error budget exhausted!');
      this.incidentManager.createIncident({
        type: 'Error Budget Exhausted',
        severity: 'Sev1',
        description: 'Error budget has been completely consumed',
        metrics: { errorBudget: this.budget }
      });
    } else if (this.budget < 0.2) {
      log('Error budget critical!');
      this.incidentManager.createIncident({
        type: 'Error Budget Critical',
        severity: 'Sev2',
        description: 'Error budget is below 20%',
        metrics: { errorBudget: this.budget }
      });
    }
  }

  getCurrentBudget() {
    return this.budget;
  }

  resetBudget() {
    const now = Date.now();
    const windowDays = SLO.ERROR_BUDGET_WINDOW;

    if ((now - this.windowStart) >= windowDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) {
      this.budget = 1.0;
      this.windowStart = now;
      log('Error budget reset for new window');
    }
  }

  calculateConsumptionRate() {
    const now = Date.now();
    const timeElapsed = (now - this.windowStart) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24); // in days
    const windowDays = SLO.ERROR_BUDGET_WINDOW;

    if (timeElapsed <= 0) return 0;

    const remainingDays = windowDays - timeElapsed;
    const consumptionRate = (1 - this.budget) / timeElapsed;

    return {
      current: consumptionRate,
      projected: consumptionRate * windowDays,
      daysRemaining: this.budget / consumptionRate
    };
  }
}

module.exports = ErrorBudget;
```

```javascript
// src/monitoring/incident-manager.js
const { MONITORING } = require('../config');
const { log } = require('./observability');
const RollbackManager = require('../rollback/rollback-manager');

class IncidentManager {
  constructor() {
    this.activeIncidents = new Map();
    this.rollbackManager = new RollbackManager();
    this.incidentCounter = 0;
  }

  async createIncident({ type, severity, description, metrics }) {
    this.incidentCounter++;
    const incidentId = `INC-${Date.now()}-${this.incidentCounter}`;

    const incident = {
      id: incidentId,
      type,
      severity,
      description,
      status: 'open',
      createdAt: new Date(),
      updatedAt: new Date(),
      metrics,
      timeline: [],
      assignedTo: null,
      resolution: null
    };

    this.activeIncidents.set(incidentId, incident);
    log(`Incident created: ${incidentId} - ${type} (${severity})`);

    // Add initial timeline entry
    this.addTimelineEntry(incidentId, 'Incident created', 'system');

    // Determine response based on severity
    await this.handleIncidentResponse(incident);

    return incidentId;
  }

  async handleIncidentResponse(incident) {
    switch (incident.severity) {
      case 'Sev1':
        await this.handleSev1Incident(incident);
        break;
      case 'Sev2':
        await this.handleSev2Incident(incident);
        break;
      case 'Sev3':
        await this.handleSev3Incident(incident);
        break;
      case 'Sev4':
        await this.handleSev4Incident(incident);
        break;
    }
  }

  async handleSev1Incident(incident) {
    // Open war room
    this.addTimelineEntry(incident.id, 'War room opened', 'system');

    // Notify stakeholders
    this.addTimelineEntry(incident.id, 'Stakeholders notified', 'system');

    // Check if automatic rollback should be triggered
    const shouldRollback = await this.rollbackManager.shouldTriggerAutomaticRollback();
    if (shouldRollback) {
      this.addTimelineEntry(incident.id, 'Automatic rollback triggered', 'system');
      await this.rollbackManager.triggerRollback('slo-violation');
    }
  }

  async handleSev2Incident(incident) {
    // Notify relevant teams
    this.addTimelineEntry(incident.id, 'Relevant teams notified', 'system');

    // Check if rollback should be considered
    const shouldRollback = await this.rollbackManager.shouldTriggerAutomaticRollback();
    if (shouldRollback) {
      this.addTimelineEntry(incident.id, 'Rollback recommended', 'system');
    }
  }

  async handleSev3Incident(incident) {
    // Add to backlog for next sprint
    this.addTimelineEntry(incident.id, 'Added to backlog for investigation', 'system');
  }

  async handleSev4Incident(incident) {
    // Add to backlog for future consideration
    this.addTimelineEntry(incident.id, 'Added to backlog for future consideration', 'system');
  }

  addTimelineEntry(incidentId, entry, author = 'system') {
    const incident = this.activeIncidents.get(incidentId);
    if (!incident) return;

    incident.timeline.push({
      timestamp: new Date(),
      entry,
      author
    });
    incident.updatedAt = new Date();

    this.activeIncidents.set(incidentId, incident);
  }

  async updateIncident(incidentId, updates) {
    const incident = this.activeIncidents.get(incidentId);
    if (!incident) return false;

    Object.assign(incident, updates);
    incident.updatedAt = new Date();

    this.addTimelineEntry(incidentId, `Incident updated: ${JSON.stringify(updates)}`, 'system');
    this.activeIncidents.set(incidentId, incident);

    return true;
  }

  async resolveIncident(incidentId, resolution) {
    const incident = this.activeIncidents.get(incidentId);
    if (!incident) return false;

    incident.status = 'resolved';
    incident.resolution = resolution;
    incident.updatedAt = new Date();

    this.addTimelineEntry(incidentId, `Incident resolved: ${resolution}`, 'system');
    this.activeIncidents.set(incidentId, incident);

    // Schedule postmortem if Sev1 or Sev2
    if (incident.severity === 'Sev1' || incident.severity === 'Sev2') {
      this.schedulePostmortem(incidentId);
    }

    return true;
  }

  schedulePostmortem(incidentId) {
    const incident = this.activeIncidents.get(incidentId);
    if (!incident) return;

    this.addTimelineEntry(
      incidentId,
      'Postmortem scheduled (to be completed within 48 hours)',
      'system'
    );

    // In a real implementation, this would create a calendar event or ticket
    log(`Postmortem scheduled for incident ${incidentId}`);
  }

  getIncident(incidentId) {
    return this.activeIncidents.get(incidentId);
  }

  getActiveIncidents() {
    return Array.from(this.activeIncidents.values());
  }

  getIncidentsBySeverity(severity) {
    return this.getActiveIncidents().filter(incident => incident.severity === severity);
  }
}

module.exports = IncidentManager;
```

```javascript
// src/monitoring/observability.js
const { SLO, MONITORING } = require('../config');
const winston = require('winston');
const { createLogger, format, transports } = winston;

// Configure logging
const logger = createLogger({
  level: 'info',
  format: format.combine(
    format.timestamp(),
    format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    new transports.Console(),
    new transports.File({ filename: 'logs/error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new transports.File({ filename: 'logs/combined.log' })
  ]
});

// Metrics storage
const metrics = {
  requests: 0,
  errors: 0,
  latency: [],
  availability: 1.0,
  canaryRequests: 0,
  canaryErrors: 0,
  canaryLatency: [],
  baselineRequests: 0,
  baselineErrors: 0,
  baselineLatency: [],
  sloViolations: 0,
  errorBudget: 1.0,
  errorBudgetConsumed: 0,
  lastUpdated: Date.now()
};

// Initialize metrics collection
setInterval(() => {
  updateAvailability();
  calculateLatencyMetrics();
}, MONITORING.METRICS_INTERVAL);

function log(message, level = 'info') {
  logger.log(level, message);
}

function recordMetric(name, value) {
  if (metrics.hasOwnProperty(name)) {
    if (Array.isArray(metrics[name])) {
      metrics[name].push(value);
      // Keep only recent metrics to prevent memory issues
      if (metrics[name].length > 100) {
        metrics[name].shift();
      }
    } else {
      metrics[name] = value;
    }
  }
  metrics.lastUpdated = Date.now();
}

function incrementMetric(name) {
  if (metrics.hasOwnProperty(name)) {
    metrics[name]++;
  }
  metrics.lastUpdated = Date.now();
}

function updateAvailability() {
  const now = Date.now();
  const timeWindow = 5 * 60 * 1000; // 5 minutes
  const recentRequests = metrics.requests - (metrics.requestsAtLastCheck || 0);
  const recentErrors = metrics.errors - (metrics.errorsAtLastCheck || 0);

  // Simple availability calculation - in production would use health checks
  const availability = recentRequests > 0
    ? 1 - (recentErrors / recentRequests)
    : 1.0;

  metrics.availability = availability;
  metrics.requestsAtLastCheck = metrics.requests;
  metrics.errorsAtLastCheck = metrics.errors;
}

function calculateLatencyMetrics() {
  if (metrics.latency.length > 0) {
    metrics.latency.sort((a, b) => a - b);
    const p95Index = Math.floor(metrics.latency.length * 0.95);
    metrics.latencyP95 = metrics.latency[p95Index] || metrics.latency[metrics.latency.length - 1];
  } else {
    metrics.latencyP95 = 0;
  }

  if (metrics.canaryLatency.length > 0) {
    metrics.canaryLatency.sort((a, b) => a - b);
    const p95Index = Math.floor(metrics.canaryLatency.length * 0.95);
    metrics.canaryLatencyP95 = metrics.canaryLatency[p95Index] || metrics.canaryLatency[metrics.canaryLatency.length - 1];
  } else {
    metrics.canaryLatencyP95 = 0;
  }

  if (metrics.baselineLatency.length > 0) {
    metrics.baselineLatency.sort((a, b) => a - b);
    const p95Index = Math.floor(metrics.baselineLatency.length * 0.95);
    metrics.baselineLatencyP95 = metrics.baselineLatency[p95Index] || metrics.baselineLatency[metrics.baselineLatency.length - 1];
  } else {
    metrics.baselineLatencyP95 = 0;
  }
}

function getCurrentMetrics() {
  return {
    requests: metrics.requests,
    errors: metrics.errors,
    errorRate: metrics.requests > 0 ? metrics.errors / metrics.requests : 0,
    latencyP95: metrics.latencyP95,
    availability: metrics.availability,
    canaryRequests: metrics.canaryRequests,
    canaryErrors: metrics.canaryErrors,
    canaryErrorRate: metrics.canaryRequests > 0 ? metrics.canaryErrors / metrics.canaryRequests : 0,
    canaryLatency: metrics.canaryLatencyP95,
    baselineRequests: metrics.baselineRequests,
    baselineErrors: metrics.baselineErrors,
    baselineErrorRate: metrics.baselineRequests > 0 ? metrics.baselineErrors / metrics.baselineRequests : 0,
    baselineLatency: metrics.baselineLatencyP95,
    sloViolations: metrics.sloViolations,
    errorBudget: metrics.errorBudget,
    errorBudgetConsumed: metrics.errorBudgetConsumed,
    canarySuccessRate: metrics.canaryRequests > 0
      ? 1 - (metrics.canaryErrors / metrics.canaryRequests)
      : 1.0,
    canaryTrafficPercentage: metrics.canaryRequests > 0
      ? (metrics.canaryRequests / (metrics.canaryRequests + metrics.baselineRequests)) * 100
      : 0
  };
}

function trackRequest(isError, latency, isCanary = false) {
  incrementMetric('requests');
  if (isCanary) {
    incrementMetric('canaryRequests');
    recordMetric('canaryLatency', latency);
  } else {
    incrementMetric('baselineRequests');
    recordMetric('baselineLatency', latency);
  }

  if (isError) {
    incrementMetric('errors');
    if (isCanary) {
      incrementMetric('canaryErrors');
    } else {
      incrementMetric('baselineErrors');
    }
  } else {
    recordMetric('latency', latency);
  }
}

module.exports = {
  log,
  recordMetric,
  incrementMetric,
  getCurrentMetrics,
  trackRequest
};
```

### 5. Load Balancing and Health Checking

```javascript
// src/load-balancing/traffic-router.js
const { INFRA } = require('../config');
const { getCurrentMetrics } = require('../monitoring/observability');
const CanaryRouter = require('../canary/canary-router');

class TrafficRouter {
  constructor() {
    this.canaryRouter = new CanaryRouter();
    this.regions = [INFRA.PRIMARY_REGION, INFRA.SECONDARY_REGION];
    this.currentRegionIndex = 0;
    this.instances = new Map();
    this.healthChecker = new HealthChecker();
  }

  async routeRequest(req) {
    // First determine if this should go to canary
    const canaryResult = await this.canaryRouter.routeRequest(req);

    // Then determine region and instance
    const region = this.getOptimalRegion();
    const instance = this.getHealthyInstance(region);

    return {
      ...canaryResult,
      region,
      instance
    };
  }

  getOptimalRegion() {
    // Simple round-robin for now - would be more sophisticated in production
    this.currentRegionIndex = (this.currentRegionIndex + 1) % this.regions.length;
    return this.regions[this.currentRegionIndex];
  }

  getHealthyInstance(region) {
    const instances = this.instances.get(region) || [];
    const healthyInstances = instances.filter(instance =>
      this.healthChecker.isInstanceHealthy(instance)
    );

    if (healthyInstances.length === 0) {
      throw new Error(`No healthy instances available in region ${region}`);
    }

    // Simple round-robin for instance selection
    const instanceIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * healthyInstances.length);
    return healthyInstances[instanceIndex];
  }

  async getCanaryMetrics() {
    return this.canaryRouter.getCanaryMetrics();
  }

  updateInstances(region, instances) {
    this.instances.set(region, instances);
  }
}

module.exports = TrafficRouter;
```

```javascript
// src/load-balancing/health-checker.js
const { SLO } = require('../config');
const { log } = require('../monitoring/observability');

class HealthChecker {
  constructor() {
    this.healthChecks = new Map();
    this.healthCheckInterval = SLO.HEALTH_CHECK_INTERVAL;
  }

  startHealthChecks() {
    setInterval(() => {
      this.performHealthChecks();
    }, this.healthCheckInterval);
  }

  async performHealthChecks() {
    for (const [instance, lastCheck] of this.healthChecks) {
      try {
        const isHealthy = await this.checkInstanceHealth(instance);
        this.healthChecks.set(instance, {
          healthy: isHealthy,
          lastChecked: Date.now(),
          lastHealthy: isHealthy ? Date.now() : lastCheck.lastHealthy
        });
      } catch (error) {
        log(`Health check failed for ${instance}: ${error.message}`);
        this.healthChecks.set(instance, {
          healthy: false,
          lastChecked: Date.now(),
          lastHealthy: lastCheck.lastHealthy
        });
      }
    }
  }

  async checkInstanceHealth(instance) {
    // In a real implementation, this would make an actual health check request
    // For this example, we'll simulate it
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      setTimeout(() => {
        // Simulate 99.9% availability
        const isHealthy = Math.random() > 0.001;
        resolve(isHealthy);
      }, 50);
    });
  }

  isInstanceHealthy(instance) {
    const check = this.healthChecks.get(instance);
    if (!check) {
      // If we've never checked, assume healthy
      return true;
    }
    return check.healthy;
  }

  async waitForHealthy(instance, retries = 3, interval = 10000) {
    for (let i = 0; i < retries; i++) {
      const isHealthy = await this.checkInstanceHealth(instance);
      if (isHealthy) {
        return true;
      }
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, interval));
    }
    return false;
  }

  async isSystemHealthy() {
    const checks = Array.from(this.healthChecks.values());
    if (checks.length === 0) return true;

    const healthyChecks = checks.filter(check => check.healthy);
    const healthRatio = healthyChecks.length / checks.length;

    return healthRatio >= 0.8; // 80% of instances healthy
  }

  registerInstance(instance) {
    this.healthChecks.set(instance, {
      healthy: true,
      lastChecked: Date.now(),
      lastHealthy: Date.now()
    });
  }

  unregisterInstance(instance) {
    this.healthChecks.delete(instance);
  }
}

module.exports = HealthChecker;
```

### 6. Main Application

```javascript
// src/app.js
const express = require('express');
const { SLO, CANARY } = require('./config');
const { trackRequest } = require('./monitoring/observability');
const SLOMonitor = require('./monitoring/slo-monitor');
const ErrorBudget = require('./monitoring/error-budget');
const CanaryDeployer = require('./canary/canary-deployer');
const CanaryMonitor = require('./canary/canary-monitor');
const RollbackManager = require('./rollback/rollback-manager');
const TrafficRouter = require('./load-balancing/traffic-router');
const HealthChecker = require('./load-balancing/health-checker');

class V9CoreApp {
  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.port = process.env.PORT || 3000;

    // Initialize components
    this.sloMonitor = new SLOMonitor();
    this.errorBudget = new ErrorBudget();
    this.canaryDeployer = new CanaryDeployer();
    this.canaryMonitor = new CanaryMonitor();
    this.rollbackManager = new RollbackManager();
    this.trafficRouter = new TrafficRouter();
    this.healthChecker = new HealthChecker();

    // Setup middleware
    this.setupMiddleware();

    // Setup routes
    this.setupRoutes();

    // Start monitoring
    this.startMonitoring();
  }

  setupMiddleware() {
    this.app.use(express.json());
    this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

    // Request tracking middleware
    this.app.use((req, res, next) => {
      const start = Date.now();
      res.on('finish', () => {
        const latency = Date.now() - start;
        const isError = res.statusCode >= 500;
        const isCanary = req.headers['x-canary-version'] !== undefined;

        trackRequest(isError, latency, isCanary);
      });
      next();
    });
  }

  setupRoutes() {
    // Health check endpoint
    this.app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
      res.status(200).json({ status: 'healthy' });
    });

    // Canary deployment endpoints
    this.app.post('/canary/deploy', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        const { version } = req.body;
        await this.canaryDeployer.startCanaryDeployment(version);
        res.status(200).json({ status: 'canary deployment started', version });
      } catch (error) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: error.message });
      }
    });

    this.app.post('/canary/promote', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        const success = await this.canaryDeployer.promoteCanary();
        if (success) {
          res.status(200).json({ status: 'canary promoted' });
        } else {
          res.status(400).json({ error: 'canary promotion failed' });
        }
      } catch (error) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: error.message });
      }
    });

    this.app.post('/canary/rollback', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        await this.canaryDeployer.rollbackCanary();
        res.status(200).json({ status: 'canary rolled back' });
      } catch (error) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: error.message });
      }
    });

    // Rollback endpoint
    this.app.post('/rollback', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        const { reason } = req.body;
        const success = await this.rollbackManager.triggerRollback(reason);
        if (success) {
          res.status(200).json({ status: 'rollback initiated' });
        } else {
          res.status(400).json({ error: 'rollback failed' });
        }
      } catch (error) {
        res.status(400).json({ error: error.message });
      }
    });

    // Metrics endpoint
    this.app.get('/metrics', (req, res) => {
      const metrics = require('./monitoring/observability').getCurrentMetrics();
      res.status(200).json(metrics);
    });

    // Main API endpoint
    this.app.all('/api/*', async (req, res) => {
      try {
        // Route the request
        const routing = await this.trafficRouter.routeRequest(req);

        // Simulate processing
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));

        // Track LLM metrics if this is an LLM request
        if (req.path.includes('/llm/')) {
          trackRequest(false, 5000, routing.isCanary); // Simulate LLM latency
        }

        res.status(200).json({
          status: 'success',
          version: routing.version,
          region: routing.region,
          instance: routing.instance,
          isCanary: routing.isCanary
        });
      } catch (error) {
        res.status(500).json({ error: error.message });
      }
    });
  }

  startMonitoring() {
    this.sloMonitor.startMonitoring();
    this.canaryMonitor.startMonitoring();
    this.healthChecker.startHealthChecks();

    // Simulate error budget consumption
    setInterval(() => {
      const metrics = require('./monitoring/observability').getCurrentMetrics();
      const errorRate = metrics.errorRate;
      if (errorRate > 0) {
        this.errorBudget.consumeBudget(errorRate * 0.0001, 'error rate');
      }
    }, 60000); // Every minute
  }

  start() {
    this.app.listen(this.port, () => {
      console.log(`V9 Core app listening on port ${this.port}`);
    });
  }
}

module.exports = V9CoreApp;
```

```javascript
// public/dashboard.js
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
  // Initialize charts
  const errorBudgetCtx = document.getElementById('errorBudgetChart').getContext('2d');
  const latencyCtx = document.getElementById('latencyChart').getContext('2d');

  const errorBudgetChart = new Chart(errorBudgetCtx, {
    type: 'line',
    data: {
      labels: [],
      datasets: [{
        label: 'Error Budget Remaining',
        data: [],
        borderColor: 'rgb(75, 192, 192)',
        tension: 0.1,
        fill: true
      }]
    },
    options: {
      responsive: true,
      scales: {
        y: {
          beginAtZero: true,
          max: 1
        }
      }
    }
  });

  const latencyChart = new Chart(latencyCtx, {
    type: 'bar',
    data: {
      labels: ['Baseline', 'Canary'],
      datasets: [{
        label: 'Latency (P95)',
        data: [0, 0],
        backgroundColor: [
          'rgba(54, 162, 235, 0.5)',
          'rgba(255, 99, 132, 0.5)'
        ],
        borderColor: [
          'rgba(54, 162, 235, 1)',
          'rgba(255, 99, 132, 1)'
        ],
        borderWidth: 1
      }]
    },
    options: {
      responsive: true,
      scales: {
        y: {
          beginAtZero: true
        }
      }
    }
  });

  // Update dashboard with real data
  function updateDashboard() {
    fetch('/metrics')
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(data => {
        // Update summary cards
        document.getElementById('availability').textContent = `${(data.availability * 100).toFixed(4)}%`;
        document.getElementById('errorBudget').textContent = `${(data.errorBudget * 100).toFixed(2)}%`;
        document.getElementById('errorBudgetProgress').style.width = `${data.errorBudget * 100}%`;

        if (data.errorBudget < 0.2) {
          document.getElementById('errorBudgetProgress').style.backgroundColor = '#ff6b6b';
        } else if (data.errorBudget < 0.5) {
          document.getElementById('errorBudgetProgress').style.backgroundColor = '#ffd93d';
        } else {
          document.getElementById('errorBudgetProgress').style.backgroundColor = '#6bcf7f';
        }

        document.getElementById('latency').textContent = `${data.latencyP95}ms`;
        document.getElementById('errorRate').textContent = `${(data.errorRate * 100).toFixed(4)}%`;

        // Update system status
        const systemStatus = document.getElementById('systemStatus');
        if (data.errorBudget <= 0) {
          systemStatus.textContent = 'ERROR BUDGET EXHAUSTED';
          systemStatus.style.backgroundColor = '#ff6b6b';
        } else if (data.errorBudget < 0.2) {
          systemStatus.textContent = 'ERROR BUDGET CRITICAL';
          systemStatus.style.backgroundColor = '#ffd93d';
        } else if (data.availability < 0.9999 || data.errorRate > 0.001 || data.latencyP95 > 300) {
          systemStatus.textContent = 'DEGRADED';
          systemStatus.style.backgroundColor = '#ffd93d';
        } else {
          systemStatus.textContent = 'HEALTHY';
          systemStatus.style.backgroundColor = '#6bcf7f';
        }

        // Update canary section
        document.getElementById('canaryTraffic').textContent = `${data.canaryTrafficPercentage.toFixed(1)}%`;
        document.getElementById('canarySuccessRate').textContent = `${(data.canarySuccessRate * 100).toFixed(2)}%`;

        // Update latency chart
        latencyChart.data.datasets[0].data = [
          data.baselineLatency,
          data.canaryLatency
        ];
        latencyChart.update();

        // Update error budget chart
        const now = new Date();
        const timeLabel = now.toLocaleTimeString();
        errorBudgetChart.data.labels.push(timeLabel);
        errorBudgetChart.data.datasets[0].data.push(data.errorBudget);

        if (errorBudgetChart.data.labels.length > 20) {
          errorBudgetChart.data.labels.shift();
          errorBudgetChart.data.datasets[0].data.shift();
        }

        errorBudgetChart.update();
      });

    // Fetch active incidents
    fetch('/incidents')
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(incidents => {
        const incidentsBody = document.getElementById('incidentsBody');
        incidentsBody.innerHTML = '';

        incidents.forEach(incident => {
          const row = document.createElement('tr');

          const severityClass = incident.severity.toLowerCase();
          row.innerHTML = `
            <td>${incident.id}</td>
            <td>${incident.type}</td>
            <td class="severity-${severityClass}">${incident.severity}</td>
            <td>${incident.status}</td>
            <td>${new Date(incident.createdAt).toLocaleString()}</td>
            <td>
              <button class="view-incident" data-id="${incident.id}">View</button>
            </td>
          `;

          incidentsBody.appendChild(row);
        });

        // Add event listeners to view buttons
        document.querySelectorAll('.view-incident').forEach(button => {
          button.addEventListener('click', function() {
            const incidentId = this.getAttribute('data-id');
            viewIncident(incidentId);
          });
        });
      });
  }

  // View incident details
  function viewIncident(incidentId) {
    fetch(`/incidents/${incidentId}`)
      .then(response => response.json())
      .then(incident => {
        alert(`
          Incident ${incident.id}
          Type: ${incident.type}
          Severity: ${incident.severity}
          Status: ${incident.status}
          Created: ${new Date(incident.createdAt).toLocaleString()}
          Description: ${incident.description}

          Timeline:
          ${incident.timeline.map(entry => `- ${new Date(entry.timestamp).toLocaleString()}: ${entry.entry}`).join('\n')}
        `);
      });
  }

  // Canary actions
  document.getElementById('startCanary').addEventListener('click', function() {
    const version = prompt('Enter canary version (e.g., v1.1.0):');
    if (version) {
      fetch('/canary/deploy', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
          'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ version })
      }).then(response => {
        if (response.ok) {
          alert('Canary deployment started');
          updateDashboard();
        } else {
          response.json().then(data => alert(`Error: ${data.error}`));
        }
      });
    }
  });

  document.getElementById('promoteCanary').addEventListener('click', function() {
    if (confirm('Are you sure you want to promote the canary deployment?')) {
      fetch('/canary/promote', {
        method: 'POST'
      }).then(response => {
        if (response.ok) {
          alert('Canary promoted');
          updateDashboard();
        } else {
          response.json().then(data => alert(`Error: ${data.error}`));
        }
      });
    }
  });

  document.getElementById('rollbackCanary').addEventListener('click', function() {
    if (confirm('Are you sure you want to rollback the canary deployment?')) {
      fetch('/canary/rollback', {
        method: 'POST'
      }).then(response => {
        if (response.ok) {
          alert('Canary rolled back');
          updateDashboard();
        } else {
          response.json().then(data => alert(`Error: ${data.error}`));
        }
      });
    }
  });

  // Initial update and set interval for updates
  updateDashboard();
  setInterval(updateDashboard, 10000); // Update every 10 seconds
});
```

### 8. Deployment Scripts

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/deploy.sh

# Exit on error
set -e

# Configuration
CANARY_PERCENTAGE=5
RAMP_UP_INTERVAL=300 # 5 minutes
MAX_CANARY_PERCENTAGE=50
STABILITY_THRESHOLD=0.999
LATENCY_THRESHOLD=1.2

# Colors for output
RED='\033[0;31m'
GREEN='\033[0;32m'
YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
NC='\033[0m' # No Color

# Function to check if canary is stable
check_stability() {
  local metrics=$(curl -s http://localhost:3000/metrics)
  local success_rate=$(echo $metrics | jq -r '.canarySuccessRate')
  local latency_ratio=$(echo $metrics | jq -r '.canaryLatency / .baselineLatency')

  echo -e "${YELLOW}Checking canary stability...${NC}"
  echo "Success rate: $success_rate (threshold: $STABILITY_THRESHOLD)"
  echo "Latency ratio: $latency_ratio (threshold: $LATENCY_THRESHOLD)"

  if (( $(echo "$success_rate < $STABILITY_THRESHOLD" | bc -l) )); then
    echo -e "${RED}Canary stability check failed: success rate too low${NC}"
    return 1
  fi

  if (( $(echo "$latency_ratio > $LATENCY_THRESHOLD" | bc -l) )); then
    echo -e "${RED}Canary stability check failed: latency too high${NC}"
    return 1
  fi

  return 0
}

# Function to promote canary
promote_canary() {
  echo -e "${GREEN}Promoting canary to production...${NC}"
  curl -s -X POST http://localhost:3000/canary/promote
  echo -e "${GREEN}Canary promoted successfully!${NC}"
}

# Function to rollback canary
rollback_canary() {
  echo -e "${RED}Rolling back canary deployment...${NC}"
  curl -s -X POST http://localhost:3000/canary/rollback
  echo -e "${RED}Canary rolled back.${NC}"
  exit 1
}

# Main deployment function
deploy() {
  local version=$1

  if [ -z "$version" ]; then
    echo -e "${RED}Error: Version not specified${NC}"
    echo "Usage: $0 <version>"
    exit 1
  fi

  echo -e "${GREEN}Starting canary deployment for version $version${NC}"

  # Start canary deployment
  curl -s -X POST -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"version\":\"$version\"}" http://localhost:3000/canary/deploy

  # Gradually increase traffic
  local current_percentage=$CANARY_PERCENTAGE
  while [ $current_percentage -lt $MAX_CANARY_PERCENTAGE ]; do
    echo -e "${YELLOW}Increasing canary traffic to $current_percentage%${NC}"

    # Check stability before increasing traffic
    if ! check_stability; then
      rollback_canary
    fi

    # Increase traffic (in a real system, this would be done via the canary router)
    current_percentage=$((current_percentage + CANARY_PERCENTAGE))

    # Wait for next ramp up
    sleep $RAMP_UP_INTERVAL
  done

  # Final stability check
  if check_stability; then
    promote_canary
  else
    rollback_canary
  fi
}

# Execute deployment
deploy $1
```

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/rollback.sh

# Exit on error
set -e

# Colors for output
RED='\033[0;31m'
GREEN='\033[0;32m'
YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
NC='\033[0m' # No Color

# Function to trigger rollback
trigger_rollback() {
  local reason=$1

  if [ -z "$reason" ]; then
    reason="manual-trigger"
  fi

  echo -e "${YELLOW}Triggering rollback: $reason${NC}"
  curl -s -X POST -H "Content-Type: application/json" -d "{\"reason\":\"$reason\"}" http://localhost:3000/rollback

  # Wait for rollback to complete
  sleep 10

  # Verify rollback
  local health_status=$(curl -s http://localhost:3000/health)
  local status=$(echo $health_status | jq -r '.status')

  if [ "$status" = "healthy" ]; then
    echo -e "${GREEN}Rollback completed successfully!${NC}"
  else
    echo -e "${RED}Rollback completed but system is not healthy!${NC}"
    exit 1
  fi
}

# Main rollback function
rollback() {
  local reason=$1

  echo -e "${RED}Starting rollback procedure...${NC}"
  trigger_rollback "$reason"
}

# Execute rollback
rollback "$1"
```

    deploy:

      timeout: 10s

volumes:

## Key Features Implemented

1. **Canary Deployments**:
   - Gradual traffic rollout with configurable percentages
   - Automatic stability checks before increasing traffic
   - Rollback mechanisms for unstable canaries
   - Monitoring of canary vs baseline metrics

2. **Automatic Rollback**:
   - Triggered by SLO violations or manual intervention
   - Different strategies for different failure scenarios
   - Health verification after rollback
   - Timeout protection

3. **SLO Monitoring**:
   - Availability, latency, and error rate tracking
   - Error budget calculation and monitoring
   - Automatic incident creation for SLO violations
   - Severity-based response protocols

4. **Observability**:
   - Comprehensive metrics collection
   - Real-time dashboard with SLO status
   - Incident tracking and management
   - Timeline and postmortem support

5. **High Availability**:
   - Multi-region deployment support
   - Health checking and automatic failover
   - Load balancing across instances
   - Graceful degradation

6. **Error Budget Management**:
   - Real-time error budget tracking
   - Automatic alerts when budget is low
   - Freeze mechanisms when budget is exhausted
   - Weekly reporting

7. **Incident Response**:
   - Severity-based incident classification
   - Automatic war room creation for Sev1/Sev2
   - Timeline tracking for postmortems
   - Blameless postmortem templates

This implementation provides a complete foundation for achieving 99.99% availability with autonomous operations. The system is designed to be self-healing with automatic rollbacks when issues are detected, and provides full observability into system health and SLO compliance.

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
Para realizar a análise de segurança e implementar autenticação e autorização robustas na V8 Core do projeto "DIYAPP Evolution - V9 Core", vamos focar nos seguintes pontos:

1. **Análise de Segurança**: 

Utilizaremos o framework STRIDE para identificar ameaças e propor correções específicas. Vamos focar em autenticação, autorização e segurança de dados.

2. **Implementação de Autenticação e Autorização**:

Optaremos por OAuth 2.0 para autenticação e RBAC (Role-Based Access Control) para autorização.

3. **Validação com Compliance**:

Garantir que todas as implementações estejam alinhadas com requisitos regulatórios de segurança.

### Passo 1: Análise de Segurança usando STRIDE
- **Spoofing**: Vamos verificar se existe alguma possibilidade de credenciais serem falsificadas. Mitigaremos isso com implementação de OAuth 2.0.
- **Tampering**: Garantimos que toda comunicação está sob TLS 1.2+ e que tokens são assinados e pode-se validar sua integridade.
- **Repudiation**: Implementaremos logs de auditoria imutáveis para todas as operações críticas de autenticação.
- **Info Disclosure**: Garantiremos que dados sensíveis estejam criptografados usando AES-256 e mascarados nos logs.
- **Denial of Service**: Implementaremos rate limiting nos endpoints de autenticação.
- **Elevation of Privilege**: Implementaremos RBAC para garantir que apenas usuários autorizados possam executar determinadas ações.

### Passo 2: Implementação

Vamos construir a estrutura de implementação usando Node.js e Express para o exemplo de API:

```bash
# Estrutura de pastas
DIYAPP-Evolution-V9-Core/
│
├── src/
│   ├── controllers/
│   ├── models/
│   ├── routes/
│   ├── middleware/
│   ├── utils/
│   └── index.js
│
├── config/
│   ├── authConfig.js
│   └── dbConfig.js
│
└── public/
    └── index.html
```

#### `config/authConfig.js`
```javascript
module.exports = {
    secret: 'your-secret-key',
    oauth: {
        clientID: 'your-oauth-client-id',
        clientSecret: 'your-oauth-client-secret',
        callbackURL: 'http://localhost:3000/auth/callback',
    }
};
```

#### `src/index.js`
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const bodyParser = require('body-parser');
const session = require('express-session');
const passport = require('passport');
const OAuth2Strategy = require('passport-oauth').OAuth2Strategy;

const app = express();

// Middleware setup
app.use(bodyParser.json());
app.use(session({ secret: 'your-session-secret', resave: false, saveUninitialized: true }));

// Load auth configuration
const authConfig = require('../config/authConfig');

// Configure OAuth2 strategy
passport.use('provider', new OAuth2Strategy({
    authorizationURL: 'https://example.com/oauth/authorize',
    tokenURL: 'https://example.com/oauth/token',
    clientID: authConfig.oauth.clientID,
    clientSecret: authConfig.oauth.clientSecret,
    callbackURL: authConfig.oauth.callbackURL
},
function(accessToken, refreshToken, profile, done) {
    // Assuming we find or create a user in our database here
    return done(null, profile);
}));

passport.serializeUser(function(user, done) {
    done(null, user);
});

passport.deserializeUser(function(obj, done) {
    done(null, obj);
});

app.use(passport.initialize());
app.use(passport.session());

// Auth route
app.get('/auth/provider', passport.authenticate('provider'));

app.get('/auth/callback', passport.authenticate('provider', { failureRedirect: '/' }),
    function(req, res) {
        res.redirect('/');
    }
);

// Example protected route
app.get('/profile', ensureAuthenticated, function(req, res) {
    res.json(req.user);
});

function ensureAuthenticated(req, res, next) {
    if (req.isAuthenticated()) { return next(); }
    res.redirect('/');
}

// Start server
app.listen(3000, () => {
    console.log('Server running on http://localhost:3000');
});
```

### Passo 3: Validação com Compliance
- Certifique-se de que toda a documentação de políticas e procedimentos de segurança esteja em conformidade com normas como LGPD e ISO 27001.
- Os logs de auditoria devem ser configurados para rastrear todas as tentativas de login e alterações de perfil de usuário.

A implementação desse exemplo abrange o esqueleto básico do uso de OAuth 2.0 para autenticação e configuração de segurança no caminho certo. É crucial validar tudo com a equipe de Compliance antes do deploy para garantir aderência regulatória completa e tratar qualquer ponto identificado em threat modeling.

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]
Para garantir que a V9 Core do projeto DIYAPP Evolution esteja em conformidade com as regulamentações de LGPD, GDPR e outras aplicáveis, precisamos implementar um conjunto de processos e controles de privacidade. Vou estruturar as diretrizes básicas em um framework de compliance para o produto, documentar processos essenciais e descrever o mapeamento de controles. Segue o código e estrutura para conformidade:

```plaintext
DIYAPP Evolution - V9 Core Compliance Framework

1. IDENTIFICAÇÃO DE DADOS:
   - Avaliar categorias de dados pessoais coletados.
   - Documentar base legal para coleta e processamento conforme LGPD e GDPR (consentimento, contrato, interesse legítimo, etc.).

2. DOCUMENTAÇÃO E REGISTROS:
   - Manter o Registro de Atividades de Processamento (ROPA) atualizado.
   - Criar uma Política de Privacidade que reflita todas as operações de tratamento de dados atuais.
   - Arquivar Avaliações de Impacto à Proteção de Dados (DPIAs) para toda feature de alto risco.

3. CONSENTIMENTO E DIREITOS DOS TITULARES:
   - Implementar consentimento granular onde a base legal seja o consentimento.
   - Automatizar o atendimento a direitos dos titulares (acesso, exclusão, correção, portabilidade).
   - Garantir um processo documentado e automatizado de solicitação de titular, respondido em até 15 dias.

4. SEGURANÇA E INCIDENTES:
   - Implementar medidas de segurança adequadas de acordo com ISO 27001.
   - Protocolo de notificação de incidente: notificação à ANPD e autoridades em 72h para incidentes significativos.
   - Manter logs de auditoria de acesso a dados pessoais sendo armazenados por no mínimo 6 meses.

5. RELACIONAMENTO COM TERCEIROS:
   - Assinar Acordos de Processamento de Dados (DPA) com todos os processadores de dados externos.
   - Garantir que provedores de LLMs não usem dados pessoais para treinamento.
   - Manter registro de processadores atualizado.

Example: Implementação de uma classe para lidar com DPIAs

```javascript
// src/compliance/DPIA.js
class DPIA {
  constructor(featureName, dataCategories, purpose, legalBasis, processors) {
    this.featureName = featureName;
    this.dataCategories = dataCategories;
    this.purpose = purpose;
    this.legalBasis = legalBasis; // Options: Consent, Contract, Legal Obligation, Legitimate Interest
    this.processors = processors;
    this.risks = [];
  }

  addRisk(description, probability, impact, mitigation) {
    this.risks.push({
      description,
      probability, // low, medium, high
      impact,      // low, medium, high
      mitigation
    });
  }

  generateReport() {
    return {
      featureName: this.featureName,
      dataCategories: this.dataCategories,
      purpose: this.purpose,
      legalBasis: this.legalBasis,
      processors: this.processors,
      risks: this.risks
    };
  }
}

module.exports = DPIA;
```

// Sample usage of the DPIA class
```javascript
// src/compliance/generateDPIAReport.js
const DPIA = require('./DPIA');

const exampleDPIA = new DPIA(
  "User Profile Update",
  ["email", "name", "address"],
  "Improving user profile accuracy",
  "Consent",
  ["Google Cloud", "Stripe"]
);

exampleDPIA.addRisk(
  "Data breach exposing user information",
  "high",
  "high",
  "Encryption at rest and in transit, regular security audits"
);

console.log(exampleDPIA.generateReport());
```

Esta abordagem permite uma estrutura clara para o compliance do projeto, garantindo que estamos em conformidade com LGPD, GDPR e outras regulamentações ao documentar nossa avaliação de impacto, manter nossos registros atualizados e implementar processos automatizados e seguros.

## 1. Configuração Inicial

### `tests/config/jest.config.js`
```javascript
module.exports = {
  preset: 'ts-jest',
  testEnvironment: 'node',
  roots: ['<rootDir>/tests'],
  testMatch: [
    '**/__tests__/**/*.+(ts|tsx|js)',
    '**/?(*.)+(spec|test).+(ts|tsx|js)'
  ],
  transform: {
    '^.+\\.(ts|tsx)$': 'ts-jest'
  },
  moduleNameMapper: {
    '^@core/(.*)$': '<rootDir>/src/core/$1',
    '^@services/(.*)$': '<rootDir>/src/services/$1',
    '^@utils/(.*)$': '<rootDir>/src/utils/$1'
  },
  collectCoverageFrom: [
    'src/**/*.{js,ts}',
    '!src/**/*.d.ts',
    '!src/**/index.ts'
  ],
  coverageThreshold: {
    global: {
      branches: 80,
      functions: 80,
      lines: 80,
      statements: 80
    },
    './src/core/': {
      branches: 90,
      functions: 90,
      lines: 90,
      statements: 90
    }
  },
  reporters: [
    'default',
    ['jest-junit', { outputDirectory: 'tests/reports', outputName: 'junit.xml' }],
    ['jest-html-reporters', {
      publicPath: 'tests/reports',
      filename: 'unit.html',
      expand: true
    }]
  ],
  setupFilesAfterEnv: ['<rootDir>/tests/config/test-setup.js']
};
```
